   <h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">
    Technology
   </h1>
   <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
    <div id="siteSub">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div>
    <div id="contentSub">
    </div>
    <div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
     Jump to:
     <a href="#mw-head">
      navigation
     </a>
     ,
     <a href="#p-search">
      search
     </a>
    </div>
    <div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en">
     <div class="hatnote" role="note">
      This article is about the use and knowledge of techniques and processes for producing goods and services. For other uses, see
      <a class="mw-disambig" href="/wiki/Technology_(disambiguation)" title="Technology (disambiguation)">
       Technology (disambiguation)
      </a>
      .
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Dampfturbine_Montage01.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2126" data-file-width="1779" height="359" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Dampfturbine_Montage01.jpg/300px-Dampfturbine_Montage01.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Dampfturbine_Montage01.jpg/450px-Dampfturbine_Montage01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Dampfturbine_Montage01.jpg/600px-Dampfturbine_Montage01.jpg 2x" width="300"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Dampfturbine_Montage01.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        A
        <a href="/wiki/Steam_turbine" title="Steam turbine">
         steam turbine
        </a>
        with the case opened. Most electricity is produced by
        <a href="/wiki/Thermal_power_station" title="Thermal power station">
         thermal power stations
        </a>
        with turbines like this one. Electricity consumption and living standards are highly correlated.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">
         <a href="#cite_note-1">
          [1]
         </a>
        </sup>
        <a href="/wiki/Electrification" title="Electrification">
         Electrification
        </a>
        was voted the most important engineering achievement of the 20th century.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2">
         <a href="#cite_note-2">
          [2]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      <b>
       Technology
      </b>
      ("science of craft", from
      <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Greek" title="Ancient Greek">
       Greek
      </a>
      <span lang="grc" xml:lang="grc">
       τέχνη
      </span>
      ,
      <i>
       techne
      </i>
      , "art, skill, cunning of hand"; and
      <span lang="grc" xml:lang="grc">
       -λογία
      </span>
      ,
      <i>
       <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/-logia" title="wikt:-logia">
        -logia
       </a>
      </i>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Liddell_1980_3-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Liddell_1980-3">
        [3]
       </a>
      </sup>
      ) is the collection of techniques,
      <a href="/wiki/Skill" title="Skill">
       skills
      </a>
      , methods and processes used in the production of
      <a href="/wiki/Good_(economics)" title="Good (economics)">
       goods
      </a>
      or
      <a href="/wiki/Service_(economics)" title="Service (economics)">
       services
      </a>
      or in the accomplishment of objectives, such as scientific investigation. Technology can be the
      <a href="/wiki/Knowledge" title="Knowledge">
       knowledge
      </a>
      of techniques, processes, etc. or it can be embedded in machines, computers, devices and factories, which can be operated by individuals without detailed knowledge of the workings of such things.
     </p>
     <p>
      The human species' use of technology began with the conversion of natural resources into simple tools. The
      <a href="/wiki/Prehistory" title="Prehistory">
       prehistoric
      </a>
      discovery of
      <a href="/wiki/Control_of_fire_by_early_humans" title="Control of fire by early humans">
       how to control fire
      </a>
      and the later
      <a href="/wiki/Neolithic_Revolution" title="Neolithic Revolution">
       Neolithic Revolution
      </a>
      increased the available sources of food and the invention of the
      <a href="/wiki/Wheel" title="Wheel">
       wheel
      </a>
      helped humans to travel in and control their environment. Developments in historic times, including the
      <a href="/wiki/Printing_press" title="Printing press">
       printing press
      </a>
      , the
      <a href="/wiki/Telephone" title="Telephone">
       telephone
      </a>
      , and the
      <a href="/wiki/Internet" title="Internet">
       Internet
      </a>
      , have lessened physical barriers to
      <a href="/wiki/Communication" title="Communication">
       communication
      </a>
      and allowed humans to interact freely on a global scale. The steady progress of
      <a href="/wiki/Military_technology" title="Military technology">
       military technology
      </a>
      has brought
      <a href="/wiki/Weapon" title="Weapon">
       weapons
      </a>
      of ever-increasing destructive power, from
      <a href="/wiki/Club_(weapon)" title="Club (weapon)">
       clubs
      </a>
      to
      <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_weapon" title="Nuclear weapon">
       nuclear weapons
      </a>
      .
     </p>
     <p>
      Technology has many effects. It has helped develop more advanced
      <a href="/wiki/Economy" title="Economy">
       economies
      </a>
      (including today's
      <a href="/wiki/Economic_globalization" title="Economic globalization">
       global economy
      </a>
      ) and has allowed the rise of a
      <a href="/wiki/Conspicuous_leisure" title="Conspicuous leisure">
       leisure class
      </a>
      . Many technological processes produce unwanted by-products, known as
      <a href="/wiki/Pollution" title="Pollution">
       pollution
      </a>
      , and deplete natural resources, to the detriment of Earth's
      <a href="/wiki/Natural_environment" title="Natural environment">
       environment
      </a>
      . Various implementations of technology influence the
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Value_(personal_and_cultural)" title="Value (personal and cultural)">
       values
      </a>
      of a society and new technology often raises new ethical questions. Examples include the rise of the notion of
      <a href="/wiki/Efficient_energy_use" title="Efficient energy use">
       efficiency
      </a>
      in terms of human
      <a href="/wiki/Productivity" title="Productivity">
       productivity
      </a>
      , a term originally applied only to machines, and the challenge of traditional norms.
     </p>
     <p>
      Philosophical debates have arisen over the use of technology, with disagreements over whether technology improves the
      <a href="/wiki/Human_condition" title="Human condition">
       human condition
      </a>
      or worsens it.
      <a href="/wiki/Neo-Luddism" title="Neo-Luddism">
       Neo-Luddism
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Anarcho-primitivism" title="Anarcho-primitivism">
       anarcho-primitivism
      </a>
      , and similar reactionary movements criticise the pervasiveness of technology in the modern world, arguing that it harms the environment and alienates people; proponents of ideologies such as
      <a href="/wiki/Transhumanism" title="Transhumanism">
       transhumanism
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Techno-progressivism" title="Techno-progressivism">
       techno-progressivism
      </a>
      view continued technological progress as beneficial to society and the human condition.
     </p>
     <p>
      Until recently, it was believed that the development of technology was restricted only to human beings, but 21st century scientific studies indicate that other
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Primates" title="Primates">
       primates
      </a>
      and certain
      <a href="/wiki/Dolphin" title="Dolphin">
       dolphin
      </a>
      communities have developed simple tools and passed their knowledge to other generations.
     </p>
     <p>
     </p>
